Bitter Thin Regular (Bitter[wght].ttf)

name

MS NID 6

MS NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.
Monotype uses NID 6 for creating CSS classes for their demo HTML. The following characters cause issues in the CSS code: '
, , , &, _, [, ], (, ), {, }, <, >, /, \, %'

NID 6 is 'Bitter-Thin', Everything looks good.

Pass

Unless you have entered into a specific license agreement granting you additional rights, your use of this software is limited by the terms of the actual license agreement you have entered into with Monotype. You may not copy or distribute this software. If you have any questions concerning your rights you should review the license agreement you received with the software. Bitter Thin Regular (Bitter[wght].ttf)

name

MS NID 16/17

MS NID 16 + NID 17 should match NID 1 (+2).
Otherwise cross platform compatibility does not work between Mac (uses NID 16+17) and Windows (uses NID 1+2). (Jan 2019)

NID 16 'Bitter' + 'Space' + NID 17 'Thin' = NID 1 'Bitter Thin'.

Pass

name

MS NID 25

Reserved word used in Variations PostScript Name Prefix NID25

Entry: 'BitterRoman'
The keyword 'Roman' may cause issues in Microsoft Office applications. Style linking and/or font embedding for MS Word won't work.
(The keyword 'Roman' causes cross platform issues in Adobe InDesign, Jan. 2019)
More infos here:
Unified Monotype Weight Name Rules

name

MS NID 6

MS NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.
Monotype uses NID 6 for creating CSS classes for their demo HTML. The following characters cause issues in the CSS code: '
, , , &, _, [, ], (, ), {, }, <, >, /, \, %'

NID 6 is 'Bitter-ThinItalic', Everything looks good.

name

MS NID 16/17

MS NID 16 + NID 17 should match NID 1 (+2).
Otherwise cross platform compatibility does not work between Mac (uses NID 16+17) and Windows (uses NID 1+2). (Jan 2019)

NID 16 'Bitter' + 'Space' + NID 17 'Thin Italic' = NID 1 'Bitter Thin' + 'Space' + NID 2 'Italic'.

Pass
